 co / tscgap9til internet kii duniya main teji se apana kadam badhaane vaale desh bharat main is samay net neutrality par bahes chhidi hui he
 The issue is so big that the Telecom Regulatory Body (TRAI) has sought a view from users by issuing a 118-page consultation
 agar aap bhi is bare main raay dena chaahate hai 24 april tak de sakate hai
 Learn all about Net Neutrality before giving an opinion: What is Net Neutrality? The term Net Neutrality was first used by Team Wu, a professor of media law at Columbia University
 net neutrality siddhanthake anusaar koi bhi sarvice pradaan karne vaali company internet ke kisi bhi contate, data or aplications ko barabari kaa darja degi
 No website and page should be blocked unless there is an unlawful fact on it
 iskaa matlab yah hua ki choti-badi sari website ko internet samaan rup se jagah degi
 Highlights related to Net Neutrality 1
 net neutrality aisa siddhant he jiske mutabik sarvice prowider company sabhi data ko samaan darja detii he
 2
 chaahe seva website visit karne kii ho yaa anya contate praapt karne kii
 3
 net neutrality kii vajah se sarvice prowider company na to data block kar sakati he or na hi uski speed slo hi kar sakati he
 4
 net neutrality na hone par main oparator data keemton ke alaava colling sarvice ke liye alag se paise vasuul sakate hai
 5
 net neutrality ko lagu nahin kiya gaya to mobile companiyaan in services ke liye alag se zyada charge bhi kar sakati hai
 Why you will be upset when Net Neutrality is removed: If Net Neutrality is not implemented, it can directly affect your pockets
 aapke paas vikalp kam ho sakate hai
 Your service provider can decide your website, news, content when and how much
 philhal aapke paas yah suvidha he ki aap internet par desi, videshi, lokapriy or alokapriy kisi bhi site ko samaan speed se hasil kar sakate hai lekin jab yah nahin rahegaa to aap sari website ko samaan speed se hasil nahin kar paaenge
 Service providers may charge you separately for whatsapp, Skype and other such features
 iske alaava company in ap kii data speed ko kam karke isaki colling sarvice ko baadhit kar sakati he
 Not implementing Net Neutrality may have the greatest impact on small business owners and entrepreneurs who have started their online businesses
 philhal ve internet ke madhyam se sidhe apane product kaa prachaar karte hai or use bechate hai
 a country like India is in dire need of it because it has been only a few years since the internet business started here and the youth are also getting jobs in this field on a large scale
 agar bijness ko thodi der ke liye chhod bhi den to yah hamaari freedom of spich ke liye bhi jaruri he
 Due to lack of net neutrality, any content can be easily blocked
 net neutrality siddhant se badi companiyaan kyon ho rahi pareshaan:skip, whatsap jaisi internet colling suvidha se telecom companiyon ke bijness par asar pad rahaa he
 Companies had raised data prices to avoid this
 pichley saal ek mobile sarvice prowider ne vioipi yani wais over internet protocol sevaaon par ek jibi data ke istemaal par 1,000 rupee tak charge lene kaa elaan kiya tha
 But he withdrew it due to criticisms
 telecom companiyaan ab bijness ke aise vikalp kii talash kar rahi he jahaan use bhi internet kii duniya se bade paimaane par kamai ho sake
 The operators want that the way the price of all the fruits in the market is not the same
 angoor santare kii apeksha zyada manhagaa miltaa he, thik usee tarah se contate or data ke hisaab se paise vasule jaaen
 Actually, this whole matter is to establish itself firmly in the market and only one will be able to establish itself in the market which will adapt the circumstances according to itself
 net neutrality ke lagu na hone se google, fasebuk, reliance, airtel, vodaphone jaisi badi companiyon kii res main ghaataa choti puunji ke bijness waalon ko hoga
 In a country like India where unemployment is the highest, the Internet has given many opportunities for youth to get employment and start through website
 agar net neutrality lagu nahin hoti he to uskaa asar rojgaar jenerate karne par bhi hoga

 "(input bhashaa se bhi) There are some tax slabs of GST for which there is tremendous dissatisfaction among the traders
 nayi kar pranali main adhiktam tex slab 28 pratishat kaa he or sarkaar ne marble-grenite udyog ko isi category main rakhaa he
 Traders are scared after hearing an increase of around 10 to 28 percent on average
 misaal ke liye marble-grenite kii stone industry
 Marble, granite, stone and tile merchants currently paying only VAT of 5 to 12 per cent in different states of the country say that the tax rate of 28% set by the GST Council has made the business already sluggish after demonetisation
 Will bring in pichley kai dinon se figsi yani federation of indian grenite and stone industry ke vyapaaree dilli main date hai
 The traders have requested the government to revise the GST rate and determine it again
 federation of indian grenite and stone industry ke rashtriya kaaryakari sadsy naresh parik ne bataaya ki 'rajasthan samet desh ke saat rajyon main pattharon ke kaam main lage kareeb 20 lakh pariwaron par jiesti ke 28 pratishat tex kii vajah se rojgaar jane kaa khatra mandara rahaa he
 Parik said that 28% GST is like a shock for traders engaged in efforts to get the business back on track after the demonetisation last year
 grenite stone ke vyapaaree pehle se hi haivi emport duty or mandi kii samasyaon se jujh rahe hai, aise main agar 5 pratishat se tex kii ye rate sidhe 28 pratishat kii gai to vyapaariyon kii qamar tut jaaegi
 He said that many traders will have to stop their business too and this is not a threat but you will see it happening in a few days ', says Lalit Rathi, founder member of Jigani Granite Industries Association in Bangalore,' Stone business The structure is such that most of our business is run on credit and sometimes payment comes in 3-6 months
 aise main har maheene ritern file karnaa or input credit se judi pechidagi hamaare liye badi mushkil kii baat hogi
 Now, if the tax rate is kept at 12 percent instead of 28, then it will be possible to do business
 'darasal marble-grenite ko 28 fisadi ke slab main rakhane ke peeche vajah ye he ki sarkaar ise lakjri item maanati he, jabaki industry kaa tark he ki marble-grenite jaisi chijen aajkal har aadmi apane ghar main istemaal kar rahaa he or ye vilasita kii vastu nahin rah gai he

 strawberry-strawberry vajan ghataane waalon ke liye sabase badhiya fal he
 They have very low carb and are also rich in antioxidants
 yues department of agriculture data (USDA) ke mutabik, 100 gram strawberry main keval 8 gram carbohydrate hoti he
 Watermelon - Watermelon is also an effective fruit for weight loss because it also contains fewer calories
 USDA ke mutabik, 100 gram tarbooz main 8 gram hi carbohydrate hoti he
 Peach can also be a good option for peach-weight loss
